information\n202: \t// (which doesn't happen by default), or when emulation-version and\n203: \t// min-compatibility-version are several versions apart so a beta or GA API\n204: \t// was being served which didn't exist at all in min-compatibility-version.\n205: \t//\n206: \t// In the alpha case - we do not support compatibility versioning of\n207: \t// alpha types and recommend users do not mix the two.\n208: \t// In the skip-level case - The version of apiserver we are retaining\n209: \t// compatibility with has no knowledge of the type,\n210: \t// so storing it in another type is no issue.\n211: \treturn binaryVersionOfResource, nil\n212: }\n213: The primary files implementing storage version registration are:\\n\\n### Files with v1beta1 to v1 Mapping\\n\\n1. **pkg/registry/authentication/rest/storage_authentication.go** - Implements `RESTStorageProvider` with methods for `v1alpha1Storage()`, `v1beta1Storage()`, and `v1Storage()`. These methods register different versions of the authentication API.\\n\\n2. **pkg/registry/storage/rest/storage_storage.go** - Contains `RESTStorageProvider` implementing storage versions for the storage API group with `v1alpha1Storage()`, `v1beta1Storage()`, and `v1Storage()` methods.\\n\\n3. **pkg/registry/admissionregistration/rest/storage_apiserver.go** - `v1Storage()` only\\n\\n## StorageVersion Manager Interface\\n\\nThe **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storageversion/manager.go** file defines the `Manager` interface (line 54) that records which resources need storage version updates and provides methods for:\\n\\n- `AddResourceInfo()` - Implements the interface with:\\n   - `resources` map storing overriding encoding configs per GroupResource\\n   - `SetResourceEncoding()` - Sets custom storage encoding for specific resources\\n   - `StorageEncodingFor()` - Returns the external storage encoding version\\n   - `InMemoryEncodingFor()` - Returns the internal storage encoding version\\n\\nThis config allows explicit mapping of v1beta1 resources to their v1 equivalents for etcd storage while maintaining backward compatibility for decoding multiple versions.\\n\\n## Integration Pattern\\n\\nThe pattern followed across all storage providers is:\\n1. Each API group has a `RESTStorageProvider` (or `StorageProvider`) struct in its rest package\\n2.
